// Define a TABLE
#VAR(Table, TABLE)
#VAR(engTable, TABLE)

// Load and activate the table
#ADDTBL("script/table.tbl", Table)
#ACTIVETBL(Table)

// Setup GBA pointers and Pointer Table
#VAR(GBA, CUSTOMPOINTER)
// Create our pointer type
